в”Ӯ bob-ags (Business Operations Butler) is a Next.js 16 call tracking and AI    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ analysis dashboard. The goal is to migrate the backend to Laravel while      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ keeping the frontend untouched, ensuring AI services (OpenRouter,            в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ AssemblyAI) continue working seamlessly.                                     в”Ӯ
